             Enjoy the historic charm of this beautiful Victorian Farmhouse with much of the original woodwork still remaining and lots of character throughout. This lovely home offers a large country kitchen with walk-through pantry, dining area with woodstove, formal living room plus family room, foyer with decorative fireplace, updated bathrooms and convenient 1st floor bedroom. On the 2nd floor, you'll find a master with a walk-in closet, sitting room plus 2 guest bedrooms; one of which is perfect for
             <span class="hide" id="util_TextFold_toggleArea">
              guests or could easily work as studio or office space. Step outside to relax on the covered porches or frolic in the gardens. Oversized barn doubles as a garage and has plenty of space for storage, workshop, garden shed and farm animals with 4 stalls. Wonderful village location within walking distance to general store and post office. Minutes to St. Albans and an easy drive to Burlington. Recent updates include a new septic in 2004, new roof in 2006, new windows, new boiler in 2012 and much more!

          <h2 data-module="zestimate">
           Zestimate Details
          </h2>
          <div class="zsg-content-component">
           <div class="zest-container">

             <div class="zest zsg-lg-1-2 zsg-md-1-1">
              <div class="zest-inner">
               <div class="zsg-g_gutterless zest-content">
                <div class=" zsg-md-1-2">
                 <div class="zest-title">
                  Zestimate
                  <span class="zsg-tooltip-launch zsg-icon-circle-question" data-target-id="zest-tip-table">
                  </span>
                  <div class="zsg-tooltip" id="zest-tip-table">
                   A
                   <strong>
                    Zestimate
                   </strong>
                   home valuation is Zillow's estimated market value. It is not an appraisal. Use it as a starting point to determine a home's value.
                   <a href="/wikipages/What-is-a-Zestimate/">
                    Learn more
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   The
                   <strong>
                    Value Range
                   </strong>
                   is the high and low estimate market value for which Zillow values a home. The more information, the smaller the range, and the more accurate the Zestimate.
                   <a href="/howto/DataCoverageZestimateAccuracy.htm">
                    See data coverage and accuracy table
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <strong>
                    Don't agree with your home's Zestimate?
                   </strong>
                   Owners can  edit their home facts  to make the Zestimate more accurate. Plus, you can leave an opinion on your Zestimate value below. Just click "Owner Estimate".
                  </div>

                  Unavailable

                   <strong>
                    Rent Zestimate
                   </strong>
                   is Zillow's estimated monthly rental price, computed using a proprietary formula. It is a starting point in determining the monthly rental price for a specific property.
                   <a href="/wikipages/What-is-a-Rent-Zestimate/">
                    Learn more
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   The
                   <strong>
                    Rent Range
                   </strong>
                   is the high and low estimate for which an apartment or home could rent. The more information we have, the smaller the range, and the more accurate the Rent Zestimate.
                   <a href="/howto/DataCoverageRentZestimateAccuracy.htm">
